:PREAMBLE:
#+title: All packages and their upstreams
#+setupfile: .orgconfig
#+name: setup
#+begin_src emacs-lisp :results silent
  (require 'emir)
#+end_src
#+name: addheader
#+header: :var header="" :var rows=""
#+begin_src elisp :hlines yes :results none
  (epkg-add-org-header rows header)
#+end_src
[[https://emacsmirror.net/stats][up]]
:END:
#+name: all-upstreams
#+begin_src emacs-lisp :results list
  (mapcar (pcase-lambda (`(,name ,url ,repopage ,homepage))
            ;; My Github Action workflows use this to clone
            ;; dependencies, so the Git url has to be favored.
            ;; https://github.com/emacscollective/workflows/blob/main/bin/install-deps
            (format "%s %s" name (or url repopage homepage "please consult a search engine")))
          (epkgs [name url repopage homepage]))
#+end_src
#+results: all-upstreams
